                    `plan_time`>0 AND `status_calender`<>'Declined', 
                    1,
                    0
                )
            ) AS `plan_task`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        `spen_time`, 
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_time`, 
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `status_calender`='accepted',
                    IF(
                        `spen_time`>0, 
                        1,
                        0
                    ),
                    0
                )
            ) AS `actual_task`,
            SUM(
                IF(
                    `project_type`='MSI Project Implementation',
                    1,
                    IF(
                        `project_type`='MSI Project Maintenance',
                        1,
                        0
                    )
                )
            ) AS `total_project` 
        FROM `sa_trx_productivity` 
        WHERE 
            `task_date` >= '2023-07-03' 
            AND `task_date` <= '2023-12-31'
